<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GENERAL MILLS REPORTS FOURTH-QUARTER AND FULL-YEAR RESULTS FOR FISCAL 2022 AND </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROVIDES FISCAL 2023 OUTLOOK </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Board of Directors Declares Six Percent Dividend Increase </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Full Year Highlights </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

6&nbsp;percent. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

was up 2&nbsp;percent. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

4&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fourth Quarter Highlights </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales increased 8&nbsp;percent to $4.9&nbsp;billion; organic net sales increased 13&nbsp;percent.
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit increased 85&nbsp;percent to $1.0&nbsp;billion; constant-currency adjusted operating profit
increased 21&nbsp;percent. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted EPS of $1.35 increased 98&nbsp;percent; adjusted diluted EPS of $1.12 were up 23&nbsp;percent in
constant currency. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS, Minn. &#150; June&nbsp;29,
2022 &#150; General Mills (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended May&nbsp;29, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Fiscal
2022 was another successful year for General Mills, marking the fourth consecutive year that we&#146;ve delivered results that met or exceeded our targets for top and bottom-line growth and cash generation,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and
Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;I am proud of the way our team advanced our Accelerate strategy this year by executing well on our core business while taking significant steps to reshape our portfolio. Though significant inflation and
supply chain disruptions put pressure on our margins, we responded quickly to address those challenges and keep our brands on shelf for our customers and consumers. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We plan to build on our strong momentum in fiscal 2023 by continuing to compete effectively, investing in our brands and capabilities,
and reshaping our portfolio. Importantly, our board reinforced its confidence in our performance and outlook by approving a six percent increase in our dividend, underlining our commitment to driving strong returns for General Mills shareholders
over the long term.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and being a force
for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures, including
seven transactions announced or completed in fiscal 2022, to further enhance its growth profile. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fourth Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 8&nbsp;percent to $4.9&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> net headwind from divestiture and acquisition activity and one point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 13&nbsp;percent. Organic net price realization and mix added
14 points to organic net sales growth, driven by Strategic Revenue Management (SRM) actions put in place in response to significant input cost inflation including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> benefit from index pricing on bakery
flour in the North America Foodservice segment. Lower organic pound volume was a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind to organic net sales growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 120 basis points to 36.2&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by higher input costs. Adjusted gross margin was down 70 basis points to 33.8&nbsp;percent of net sales,
driven by double-digit input cost inflation, higher other cost of goods sold, and supply chain deleverage, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $1.0&nbsp;billion was up 85&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by higher gross profit
dollars, lower restructuring charges, and divestiture gains, partially offset by unfavorable net investment activity.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 20.8&nbsp;percent was up 870 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit increased
21&nbsp;percent, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars and lower adjusted selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin increased 200 basis points to 18.3&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> were up 97&nbsp;percent to $823&nbsp;million and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 98&nbsp;percent to $1.35, driven primarily by higher operating profit and lower average diluted shares outstanding. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.12 increased 23&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted
operating profit and lower average diluted shares outstanding. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Full Year Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 5&nbsp;percent to $19.0&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> net headwind from divestiture and acquisition activity. Organic net sales increased 6&nbsp;percent. Organic net price realization and mix added 7 points to organic net sales growth, driven by SRM
actions put in place in response to significant input cost inflation including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from index pricing on bakery flour in the North America Foodservice segment. Lower organic pound volume was a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind to organic net sales growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 190 basis points to 33.7&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs,
partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross margin was down 180 basis points to 33.0&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by 8&nbsp;percent annual input cost inflation, higher other cost of goods sold, and supply chain
deleverage, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $3.5&nbsp;billion was up 11&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by gains on divestitures
and lower restructuring charges, partially offset by unfavorable net investment activity.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 18.3&nbsp;percent was up 100 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit increased 2&nbsp;percent, driven by
lower adjusted SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin decreased 50 basis points to 16.9&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> were up 16&nbsp;percent to $2.7&nbsp;billion and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 17&nbsp;percent to $4.42, primarily reflecting higher operating profit, a lower effective tax rate, and lower average diluted shares outstanding. Adjusted diluted EPS of $3.94 was up 4&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven
primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, lower net interest expense, and lower average diluted shares outstanding, partially offset by lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> benefit plan income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Portfolio Reshaping </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills took important steps to advance its portfolio reshaping efforts during fiscal 2022, announcing or closing seven transactions that are expected to
increase the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-</FONT> and bottom-line growth profile over the long term. These include the acquisition of the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>True Chews</I>, and <I>Top Chews</I> pet treats brands in North
America, which closed in the first quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of yogurt in Europe, which closed in the second quarter of fiscal 2022; a series of divestitures of dough in Europe and Israel, which closed between the third quarter of
fiscal 2022 and the first quarter of fiscal 2023; the acquisition of the TNT Crust foodservice pizza crust business in North America, which closed in the first quarter of fiscal 2023; and the prospective divestiture of the <I>Helper</I> main meals
and <I>Suddenly Salad</I> side dishes businesses in North America, which is expected to close in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Operating
Segment Results </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Note: Tables may not foot due to rounding. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR STYLE="font-size:1px; ">
<TD VALIGN="bottom"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; border-top:3.00px double #000000">&nbsp;</P></TD>

</TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment increased 11&nbsp;percent to $3.0&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were also up 11&nbsp;percent. Net sales were up 18&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks, up 14&nbsp;percent in U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions, up 5&nbsp;percent in U.S.
Morning Foods, and down 1&nbsp;percent in Canada. Segment operating profit of $764&nbsp;million was up 18&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher
input costs and lower volume. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, North America Retail segment net sales increased 3&nbsp;percent to $11.6&nbsp;billion.
Net price realization and mix added 9 points to net sales growth, driven by SRM actions put in place in response to significant input cost inflation. Pound volume was a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> headwind to net sales growth.
Organic net sales were also up 3&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $2.7&nbsp;billion was down 1&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume, partially offset by favorable net
price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the Pet segment increased 37&nbsp;percent to $610&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and pound volume
growth. Net sales results in the quarter included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">15-point</FONT> benefit from the pet treats acquisition. Organic net sales were up 22&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 10&nbsp;percent to
$113&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume, including benefits from the pet treats acquisition, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, Pet segment net sales increased 30&nbsp;percent to $2.3&nbsp;billion. Net price realization and mix added 19 points to net
sales growth, including 9 points of favorable mix from the pet treats acquisition and the impact of SRM actions put in place in response to input cost inflation. Pound volume added 11 points to net sales growth, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> benefit from the pet treats acquisition. Organic net sales were up 18&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 13&nbsp;percent to $471&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price
realization and mix and higher volume, including benefits from the pet treats acquisition, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net
sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 25&nbsp;percent to $526&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">16-point</FONT> benefit from market index pricing on
bakery flour, partially offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were also up 25&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 23&nbsp;percent to $81&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by
higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, North America Foodservice net sales increased 24&nbsp;percent to
$1.8&nbsp;billion. Net price realization and mix added 19 points to net sales growth, driven by 11 points from market index pricing on bakery flour and other SRM actions put in place in response to significant input cost inflation. Pound volume
added 5 points to net sales growth. Organic net sales were also up 24&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 26&nbsp;percent to $256&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume, partially offset by
higher input costs. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales for the International segment were down 21&nbsp;percent to $750&nbsp;million, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">25-point</FONT> headwind from the divestitures of the European yogurt and dough businesses and 2 points of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of
$76&nbsp;million was up 36&nbsp;percent as reported and up 40&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by lower volume, including the impact of the
European yogurt and dough divestitures, and higher input costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year, International net sales declined 9&nbsp;percent to
$3.3&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-point</FONT> headwind from the divestitures of the European yogurt and dough businesses and 1 point of favorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales were up 2&nbsp;percent,
driven by favorable organic net price realization and mix. Segment operating profit of $232&nbsp;million was down 2&nbsp;percent as reported and down 4&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume,
including the impact of the European yogurt and dough divestitures, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth-quarter net sales
for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results in constant currency, driven by positive net price realization and mix, offset by lower volume. Constant-currency net sales increased
6&nbsp;percent for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ) in the quarter, driven by strong core performance and improved distribution. Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint
ventures in the quarter were $20&nbsp;million compared to $28&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by lower profit at CPW. For the full year, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures decreased
5&nbsp;percent to $112&nbsp;million. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-year</FONT> compound growth basis, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from
joint ventures were up 16&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Full-year unallocated corporate items totaled $403&nbsp;million net expense compared to $212&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $445&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to
$428&nbsp;million net expense last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded a net $194&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT>
gain on divestitures in fiscal 2022 compared to a $54&nbsp;million loss a year ago <I>(please see Note 2 below for more information on these items)</I>. Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled a $26&nbsp;million net recovery this
year compared to a $170&nbsp;million expense a year ago <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these charges)</I>. <I></I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense in fiscal 2022 totaled $380&nbsp;million compared to $420&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by lower average debt
balances. The effective tax rate for fiscal 2022 was 18.3&nbsp;percent compared to 22.0&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 6 below for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was 20.9&nbsp;percent
compared to 21.1&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net earnings attributable to redeemable and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interests totaled $28&nbsp;million in fiscal 2022 compared to $6&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by the loss on the sale of the Latic&iacute;nios Carolina yogurt business in Brazil in
fiscal 2021, partially offset by the sale of the company&#146;s interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl in fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2022
cash provided by operating activities increased 11&nbsp;percent to $3.3&nbsp;billion, driven primarily by higher net earnings. Capital investments of $569&nbsp;million were up 7&nbsp;percent from a year ago. Full-year operating cash flow conversion
was 121&nbsp;percent of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings and free cash flow conversion was 113&nbsp;percent of adjusted <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings. Dividends paid essentially matched <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels at $1.2&nbsp;billion. General Mills repurchased approximately 14&nbsp;million shares of common stock in fiscal 2022 for a total of $877&nbsp;million compared to $301&nbsp;million in share repurchases
a year ago. Average diluted shares outstanding decreased 1&nbsp;percent to 613&nbsp;million. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Dividend Increase </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The General Mills board of directors declared a quarterly dividend of $0.54 per share, payable August&nbsp;1, 2022, to shareholders of record July&nbsp;8,
2022. This represents a 6&nbsp;percent increase from the previous quarterly rate of $0.51 per share. General Mills and its predecessor company have paid dividends without interruption for 123 years. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2023 Outlook </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills expects the
largest factors impacting its performance in fiscal 2023 will be the economic health of consumers, the inflationary cost environment, and the frequency and severity of disruptions in the supply chain. The company anticipates double-digit inflation
on its cost of goods sold in fiscal 2023 and is addressing inflation headwinds with HMM cost savings and net price realization generated through its SRM capability. The company is planning for volume elasticities to increase but remain below
historical levels and supply chain disruptions to slowly moderate in fiscal 2023 compared to fiscal 2022 levels. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills has
announced a series of portfolio reshaping transactions over the past year that are expected to increase the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-</FONT> and bottom-line growth profile over the long term. The company estimates the net
impact of these transactions will reduce fiscal 2023 adjusted operating profit growth and adjusted diluted EPS growth by approximately 3&nbsp;percent each, driven by the impact of foregone operating profit and stranded costs related to the divested
businesses, partially offset by incremental profit from the acquired businesses. The company expects the net proceeds from the divestitures will support an increased share repurchase plan in fiscal 2023, resulting in a 2 to 3&nbsp;percent net
reduction in its average diluted share count for the year, which is above its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">long-run</FONT> target of a 1 to 2&nbsp;percent annual net share count reduction. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With these assumptions in mind, General Mills outlined its key full-year fiscal 2023 financial targets: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

constant currency from the base of $3.2&nbsp;billion reported in fiscal 2022, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestitures and acquisitions announced or closed in fiscal 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

activities, pricing actions, and promotional activities of our competitors; economic conditions, including changes in inflation rates, interest rates, tax rates, or the availability of capital; product development and innovation; consumer acceptance
of new products and product improvements; consumer reaction to pricing actions and changes in promotion levels; acquisitions or dispositions of businesses or assets; changes in capital structure; changes in the legal and regulatory environment,
including tax legislation, labeling and advertising regulations, and litigation; impairments in the carrying value of goodwill, other intangible assets, or other long-lived assets, or changes in the useful lives of other intangible assets; changes
in accounting standards and the impact of significant accounting estimates; product quality and safety issues, including recalls and product liability; changes in consumer demand for our products; effectiveness of advertising, marketing, and
promotional programs; changes in consumer behavior, trends, and preferences, including weight loss trends; consumer perception of health-related issues, including obesity; consolidation in the retail environment; changes in purchasing and inventory
levels of significant customers; fluctuations in the cost and availability of supply chain resources, including raw materials, packaging, energy, and transportation; effectiveness of restructuring and cost saving initiatives; volatility in the
market value of derivatives used to manage price risk for certain commodities; benefit plan expenses due to changes in plan asset values and discount rates used to determine plan liabilities; failure or breach of our information technology systems;

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal year ends on the last Sunday in May. Fiscal years
2022 and 2021 consist of 52 weeks, while fiscal 2020 consisted of 53 weeks. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As part of a long-term plan to conform the fiscal year ends of
all our operations, in fiscal 2020 we changed the reporting period of our Pet segment from an April fiscal <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> to a May fiscal <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> to match our fiscal
calendar. Accordingly, our fiscal 2020 results include 13 months of Pet segment results compared to 12 months in fiscal 2022 and 2021. The impact of this change was not material to our consolidated results of operations and, therefore, we did not
restate prior period financial statements for comparability. Our India business is on an April fiscal year end. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022, we entered into a definitive agreement to acquire TNT Crust. The
transaction closed subsequent to the end of the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022,
we entered into a definitive agreement to sell our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business to Eagle Family Foods Group for approximately $610&nbsp;million. We expect to close the divestiture in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. We
have classified all related assets as held for sale in our Consolidated Balance Sheets as of May&nbsp;29, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the third quarter
of fiscal 2022, we sold our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) in exchange for Sodiaal&#146;s interest in our Canadian yogurt business, a modified agreement for
the use of Yoplait and Libert&eacute; brands in the United States and Canada, and cash. We recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $164&nbsp;million on the sale of these businesses including an additional net <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $15&nbsp;million related to purchase price adjustments in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2022, we acquired Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the
transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business into our Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $762&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the
Nudges, Top Chews, and True Chews brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer relationship asset of $40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet reporting unit and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro
forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021, we recorded a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> loss of $54&nbsp;million related to the sale of our Latic&iacute;nios Carolina business in Brazil. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2022, we approved restructuring actions in the International segment to drive efficiencies in
manufacturing and logistics operations. We expect to incur approximately $21&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and project-related costs related to these actions, of which approximately $12&nbsp;million will be cash. These charges are expected
to consist of approximately $8&nbsp;million of severance and $10&nbsp;million of other costs, primarily asset write-offs. We also expect to incur approximately $3&nbsp;million of project-related costs. We recognized $8&nbsp;million of severance and
$7&nbsp;million of other costs in fiscal 2022. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2024. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As a result of shifts in the composition of estimated expenses related to our previously
announced global organizational structure and resource realignment actions, we recorded a $34&nbsp;million reduction to our restructuring reserves as of May&nbsp;29, 2022, primarily related to estimated severance charges. We expect these actions to
incur total restructuring charges of approximately $125&nbsp;million to $135&nbsp;million, of which we expect approximately $100&nbsp;million to be severance and $30&nbsp;million of other costs. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of
fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2021, we approved restructuring actions designed to better align our organization structure and resources with
strategic initiatives and recognized $157&nbsp;million of restructuring charges, consisting of $149&nbsp;million of severance and other benefits costs and $8&nbsp;million of other costs. In fiscal 2021, we also approved restructuring actions to
leverage more efficient and effective <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">route-to-market</FONT></FONT> models and to optimize our supply chain in our International segment and recognized $13&nbsp;million of
restructuring charges related to these actions, consisting of $9&nbsp;million of severance costs and $4&nbsp;million of other costs. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(4)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022, unallocated corporate expense decreased $40&nbsp;million to
$74&nbsp;million compared to $114&nbsp;million last year. We recorded a $117&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuations of certain
commodity positions and grain inventories in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022, compared to a $21&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. In fiscal 2022, we recorded $36&nbsp;million of net losses related to the
sale of corporate investments and valuation adjustments, compared to $2&nbsp;million of net losses in fiscal 2021. We recorded $2&nbsp;million of integration costs related to acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business and $16&nbsp;million
of transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl, the definitive agreements to sell our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business, and
definitive agreement to acquire TNT Crust in fiscal 2022, compared to $9&nbsp;million of transaction costs in fiscal 2021. In addition, we recorded a $2&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item in fiscal 2022 compared to a
$9&nbsp;million recovery in fiscal 2021. In fiscal 2021, we recorded a $3&nbsp;million favorable adjustment related to a product recall in fiscal 2020 in our international Green Giant business. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In fiscal 2022, unallocated corporate expense increased $191&nbsp;million to $403&nbsp;million compared to $212&nbsp;million last year. In
fiscal 2022, we recorded a $133&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories, compared
to a $139&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the prior year. In fiscal 2022, we recorded $15&nbsp;million of net losses related to the sale of corporate investments and valuation adjustments, compared to $76&nbsp;million of net gains in fiscal
2021. We recorded $22&nbsp;million of integration costs related to our acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business and $73&nbsp;million of transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC,
and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl, the definitive agreements to sell our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business, and definitive agreement to acquire TNT Crust in fiscal 2022 compared to $10&nbsp;million of transaction costs
in fiscal 2021. In addition, we recorded a $22&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item in fiscal 2022 compared to a $9&nbsp;million recovery in fiscal 2021. We recorded a $13&nbsp;million insurance recovery in fiscal 2022. In
fiscal 2021, we recorded a $4&nbsp;million favorable adjustment related to a product recall in fiscal 2020 in our international Green Giant business. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022 was 14.3&nbsp;percent compared to
22.3&nbsp;percent for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021. The 8.0 percentage point decrease was primarily due to a change in valuation allowance on our capital loss carryforward, certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-taxable</FONT> components
of the divestiture gains, and certain unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> discrete tax items in fiscal 2021. Our adjusted effective tax rate was 19.0&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to
18.5&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see Note 7 below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for fiscal 2022 was 18.3&nbsp;percent compared to 22.0&nbsp;percent in fiscal 2021. The 3.7 percentage point decrease
was primarily due to a change in valuation allowance on our capital loss carryforward, certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-taxable</FONT> components of the divestiture gains, and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction. Our
adjusted effective tax rate was 20.9&nbsp;percent in fiscal 2022, compared to 21.1&nbsp;percent in the same period of fiscal 2021 (see Note 7 below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. For each of these <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an
explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our consolidated net sales and segment net sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board
of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes. We believe that organic net sales growth rates provide useful information to investors
because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd&nbsp;week, when applicable, have on <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results
above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present
this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal
year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency
exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying
performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange
markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Also, certain measures in this release are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from
infrequently occurring events or items that, in management&#146;s judgment, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2023 outlook for organic net sales growth, constant-currency adjusted operating profit, adjusted diluted EPS, and free cash flow are
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, restructuring charges and
project-related costs, acquisition transaction and integration costs, acquisitions, divestitures, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects. We are not able to reconcile these
forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measures without unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of
certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates and commodity prices or the timing or impact of acquisitions, divestitures, and restructuring actions throughout fiscal 2023. The unavailable information could have a
significant impact on our fiscal 2023 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2023, we currently expect: foreign currency exchange rates (based
on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and acquisitions and divestitures completed prior to fiscal 2023 and those closed or expected to close in fiscal 2023 to reduce net sales growth by approximately 3&nbsp;percent; foreign
currency exchange rates to reduce adjusted operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth by approximately 1&nbsp;percent; and restructuring charges and project-related costs and transaction and acquisition integration costs related to actions
previously announced to total approximately $15&nbsp;million to $25&nbsp;million. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures (gain) loss</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Divestitures gain related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale
of our European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Divestiture loss related to the sale of our Latic&iacute;nios Carolina business in Brazil in fiscal 2021. Please see Note 2. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal
2022 transaction costs relate primarily to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl, the sale of our European dough businesses, the definitive agreements to sell our Helper main meals and
Suddenly Salad side dishes business, and the definitive agreement to acquire TNT Crust. Fiscal 2021 transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the
acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business. Please see Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax
recovery</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022 and fiscal 2021. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments and the gain on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2022 and fiscal 2021. Valuation adjustments and the loss
on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2020. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring (recoveries) charges</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges for International supply chain optimization actions and net restructuring recoveries for previously announced
restructuring actions in fiscal 2022. Restructuring charges for previously announced restructuring actions in fiscal 2021 and fiscal 2020. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Product
recall adjustment recorded in fiscal 2021 related to a recall in our international Green Giant business in fiscal 2020. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring charges</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Tax items</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Discrete tax
benefit recognized in fiscal 2022 related to a release of a valuation allowance associated with our capital loss carryforwards expected to be used against future divestiture gains. Discrete tax item related to amendments to reorganize certain U.S.
retiree health and welfare benefits plans in fiscal 2021. Discrete tax benefit related to the reorganization of certain wholly owned subsidiaries in fiscal 2020. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth on a Constant-currency Basis </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted operating
profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Diluted EPS and Related Constant-currency Growth Rate </U></P>

because it is the profitability measure we use to evaluate earnings performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it provides transparency to underlying performance of our segments by excluding
the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Effective Income Tax Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe this measure provides useful information to investors because it presents the adjusted effective income tax rate on a comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted effective income tax rates are calculated as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
